import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch


def get_es():
    es = Elasticsearch(
        hosts=[{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}],
        http_auth=('elastic', '<PASSWORD>'),
        scheme=""https"",
        retry_on_timeout=True,
        max_retries=10
    )

    return es


def search_by_field_name(es):
    # Search by field name
    body = {
        ""query"": {
            ""match"": {""VAERS_ID"": ""138564""}
        }
    }
    res = es.search(index='vaersdata', doc_type='_doc', body=body)
    print(""Got %d Hits:"" % res['hits']['total'])
    for hit in res['hits']['hits']:
        print(""%(timestamp)s %(author)s: %(text)s"" % hit[""_source""])"

    This function takes in a question string and returns the condition value of that question.

    ""size"": 0,
    ""_source"": [""STATE""],
    ""aggs"" : {
        ""group_by_state"" : {
            ""terms"" : {
                ""field"" : ""STATE"",

            }
        }
    }
}

# Get the buckets from the response
buckets = res['aggregations']['group_by_state']['buckets']

# Print the bucket keys (states)
print(""States:"")
for bkt in buckets:
    print(bkt['key'])

11209,"'''

def get_condition(question):
    if 'in' not in question:
        return None

    tokens = question.split()
    idx = tokens.index('in') + 1
    return "" "".join(tokens[idx:])


def generate_query(field_name, condition_value=None):
    if condition_value == None or len(condition_value) < 3:
        return {
            ""match"": {
                field_name: {
                    ""query"": ""*""
                }
            }
        }
    
    return {
        ""bool"": {
            ""must"": [{
                ""match"": {
                    field_name: {
                        ""query"": ""*""
                    }
                }
            }, {
                ""match"": {
                    f""{field_name}.keyword"": {
                        ""query"": condition_value
                    }
                }
            }]
        }
    }

from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


def get_most_popular_ra(index):
    """"""
    This function returns the most popular ra in a given index of the database

    Parameters
    ----------
    index : str
        Name of the index to search
    
    Returns
    -------
    dict
        Dictionary containing the most popular ra and their counts
    """"""
    body = {
        ""size"":0, 
        ""_source"":[""VAERS_ID"", ""RECVDATE""],
        ""aggs"":{
            ""ra"":{""terms"":{""field"":""ASSIGNED_TO"",""size"":10}}
        }
    }
    res = es.search(index=index, body=body)
    return res['aggregations']['ra']['buckets']

4917,"'''

def get_condition(question):
    '''
    This function takes in a question string and returns the condition value of the field. 
    For example, if the question is ""What is the condition value for this field?"" it will return the answer to the question.
    '''
    # split the question into words
    words = question.split()

    # find the index of the word 'value'
    idx = words.index('value')
    
    # get the next word after 'value'
    condition = words[idx+1]

    return condition


def generate_query(field_name, condition):
    '''
    This function generates an Elasticsearch query given the field name and condition value.
    '''
    # create the base query
    query = {
        ""size"": 0, 
        ""_source"": [""RECVDATE"", ""STATE"", ""AGE_YRS"", ""VAERS_ID"", ""SEX"", ""SYMPTOM_TEXT"", ""DI"

5092,"'''

def get_condition(question):
    '''
    This function takes in a question string and returns the condition value

    Parameters
    ----------
    question : str
        Question string to be parsed
    
    Returns
    -------
    condition : str
        Condition value extracted from the question string
    '''
    # split the question into words
    words = question.split()
    # find the index where 'is' occurs
    idx = words.index('is')
    # return the word after 'is' as the condition value
    condition = words[idx+1]
    return condition


def generate_query(field_name, condition):
    '''
    This function generates an Elasticsearch query given a field name and 
    condition value

    Parameters
    ----------
    field_name : str
        Field name to search for
    condition : str
        Condition value to filter by
    
    Returns
    -------
    query : dict
        Dictionary containing the Elasticsearch query
    '''
    # create the base query
    query = {
        """

def get_condition(question):
    '''
    This function takes in a question string and returns the condition value

    Parameters
    ----------
    question : str
        Question string that needs to be parsed
    
    Returns
    -------
    condition : str
        Condition value extracted from the question string
    '''
    # split the question into words
    words = question.split()
    # find the index of the word 'is'
    idx = words.index('is')
    # return the condition value
    condition = "" "".join(words[(idx+1):])
    return condition


def generate_query(field_name, condition):
    '''
    This function generates an Elasticsearch query given a field name and 
    condition value

    Parameters
    ----------
    field_name : str
        Field name that will be used as the basis for the Elasticsearch 
        query
    condition : str
        Condition value that will be used as the basis for the Elasticsearch 
        query
    
    Returns
    -------
    query : dict"
5610,"'''

def get_condition(question):
    '''
    This function takes in a question string and returns the condition value

    Parameters
    ----------
    question : str
        Question string that needs to be parsed
    
    Returns
    -------
    condition : str
        Condition value extracted from the question string
    '''
    # split the question into words
    words = question.split()
    # find the index of the word 'is'
    idx = words.index('is')
    # return the condition value which is the next word after 'is'
    condition = words[idx+1]
    return condition


def generate_query(field_name, condition):
    '''
    This function generates an Elasticsearch query given the field name and 
    condition value

    Parameters
    ----------
    field_name : str
        Field name extracted from the prompt
    condition : str
        Condition value extracted from the question string
    
    Returns
    -------
    query : dict
        Dictionary containing the Elasticsearch query
    '''
    # create the"

def get_condition(question):
    if 'dignose' in question or 'disease' in question:
        return 'DIED'
    elif 'incontinent' in question or 'incontinence' in question:
        return 'L_THREAT'
    else:
        return None

    # print('Question:', question)
    # print('Condition:', condition)

        condition = get_condition(question)

        return ''

def get_condition(question):
    '''
    This function takes in a question string and returns the condition value 
    associated with that question. For example, if the question was ""What is the 
    condition value for this field?"" Then it would return the answer to that question.
    '''
    
    # Split the question into words
    split = question.split()

    # Get the index of the word 'value'
    idx = split.index('value')

    # Return the word after the word 'value'
    return split[idx + 1]


def generate_query(field_name, condition_value):

    corresponding condition value.

        ""size"": 0,
        ""_source"": [""*""],
        ""query"": {
            ""bool"": {
                ""must"": []
            }
        },

Answer:
{
    ""query"": {
        ""bool"": {
            ""must"": [
                {
                    ""term"": {
                        ""DIED"": true
                    }
                },
                {
                    ""term"": {
                        ""HOSPITAL"": true
                    }
                }
            ]
        }
    }
}

def get_condition(question):
    '''
    This function takes in a question string and returns the condition value of that question. 
    For example, if the input was ""What is the condition value for this field?"" it would return ""[ ]""
    '''
    # Split the question into two parts at the colon
    split = question.split(':')
    
    # Return the second part (the condition)
    return split[-1]


def generate_elasticsearch_query(field_name, condition_value):
    '''
    This function takes in a field name and a condition value and generates an Elasticsearch query.
    It will be used to find the documents containing the condition value within the specified field.
    '''
    # Create the base query
    query = {
       'size': 0, 
        '_source': ['RECVDATE', 'STATE', 'AGE_YRS', 'VAERS_ID', 'SEX', 'SYMPTOM_TEXT', '"

### Give me all the patients who is 12.0 years old or older than 35.0 years old.
Answer:
{
    ""query"": {
        ""bool"": {
            ""should"": [
                {""range"": {""AGE_YRS"": {""gte"": 12}}},
                {""range"": {""AGE_YRS"": {""lte"": 35}}}
            ],
            ""minimum_should_match"": 1
        }
    }
}

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch


def get_es():
    es = Elasticsearch(
        hosts=[{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}],
        http_auth=('elastic', '<PASSWORD>'),
        scheme=""https"",
        retry_on_timeout=True,
        max_retries=10
    )

    return es


def search_by_field_name(es):
    # Search by field name
    body = {
        ""query"": {
            ""match"": {""FIELD_NAME"": ""CONDITION_VALUE""}
        }
    }
    res = es.search(index='clinical-notes', doc_type='_doc', body=body)
    print(""Got %d Hits:"" % res['hits']['total'])
    for hit in res['hits']['hits']:
        print(""%(timestamp)s %(author)s: %(text)s"" % hit[""_source""])

if __name__ == ""__main__"":
    print(""Welcome to the Covid-19 Chatbot!"")
    while True:
        try:
            question = input(""\nPlease enter your question or type 'quit' to exit:\n"")

            if question.lower() == ""quit"":
                break

            answer = get_answer(question)
            print(f""Chatbot's response: {answer}"")

        except Exception as e:
            print(e)"
7782,"""""""
import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


def get_all_documents(index):
    """"""
    This function returns a list of documents in the index passed as parameter

    :param index: Index name
    :return: List of documents
    """"""
    res = es.search(
        index=index,
        body={
            ""query"": {
                ""match_all"": {}
            }
        },
        size=10000)
    return res['hits']['hits']


def get_document_by_id(_id, index):
    """"""
    This function returns a document by id

    :param _id: Document ID
    :param index: Index name
    :return: Document
    """"""
    res = es.get(index=index, doc_type='doc', id=_id)
    return res['_source']


def search_by_field_value(field_name, field_value, index"

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch


def get_es():
    es = Elasticsearch(
        hosts=[{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}],
        http_auth=('elastic', '<PASSWORD>'),
        scheme=""https"",
        retry_on_timeout=True,
        max_retries=10
    )

    return es


def search_by_field_name(es):
    # Search by field name
    body = {
        ""query"": {
            ""match"": {""STATE"": ""TX""}
        }
    }
    res = es.search(index='vaersdata', doc_type='_doc', body=body)
    print(""Got %d Hits:"" % res['hits']['total'])
    for hit in res['hits']['hits']:
        print(""%(timestamp)s %(author)s: %(text)s"" % hit[""_source""])

7846,"""""""
import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch


def get_es():
    es = Elasticsearch(
        hosts=[{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}],
        http_auth=('elastic', '<PASSWORD>'),
        scheme=""https"",
        retry_on_timeout=True,
        max_retries=10
    )

    return es


def search_by_field_name(es):
    # Search by field name
    body = {
        ""query"": {
            ""match"": {""FIELD_NAME"": ""CONDITION_VALUE""}
        }
    }
    res = es.search(index='clinical-notes', doc_type='_doc', body=body)
    print(""Got %d Hits:"" % res['hits']['total'])
    for hit in res['hits']['hits']:
        print(""%(timestamp)s %(author)s: %(text)s"" % hit[""_source""])

def get_condition(question):
    '''
    This function takes in a question string and returns the condition value of that question. 
    For example, if the input is ""What is the condition value for this field?"" it will return the answer to the question.
    '''
    # TODO: Write your code here
    condition = """"
    if 'What' in question:
        condition = question.split('is')[2].strip()
    elif 'Which' in question:
        condition = question.split('is')[2].strip()
    else:
        condition = question.split('are')[1].strip()

    return condition

                {""match"": {""DIED"": ""N""}},

            ],
            ""filter"": [{""term"": {""VAX_NAME"": ""COVID-19 mRNA (nucleoside modified)""}},{""term"": {""VAX_TYPE"": ""COMIRNATY PENTAVALENT (CPV) VACCINE""}}]
        }
    },
    ""_source"": [""RECVDATE"", ""STATE"", ""AGE_YRS"", ""VAERS_ID"", ""SEX"", ""SYMPTOM_TEXT"", ""DIED"", ""ER_VISIT"", ""L_THREAT"", ""HOSPITAL"", ""HOSPDAYS"", ""DISABLE"", ""VAX_DATE"", ""LAB_DATA"", ""OTHER_MEDS"", ""CUR"
9659,"'''

def get_condition(question):
    '''
    This function takes in a string of text and returns the condition value 
    associated with that string.
    
    Parameters:
        question (str) - String containing the question to be parsed
        
    Returns: 
        condition (str) - String containing the condition value associated with the inputted question
    '''
    # Create an empty list to store the conditions
    conditions = []

    # Split the question into individual words
    split_question = question.split()

    # Loop through each word in the question
    for i in range(len(split_question)):

        # If the word contains 'is', it's probably a condition
        if ""is"" in split_question[i]:

            # Add the next word to the list
            conditions.append(split_question[i+1])
            
    return conditions


def generate_query(field_name, condition_value):
    '''
    This function generates an Elasticsearch query given a field"
9664,"{
    ""query"": {
        ""match"": {
            ""RECVDATE"": ""02/23/2022""
        }
    }
}
